I was on m y way to Reno from Santa Rosa and needed a car wash so we stopped on the way.

I was really impressed with every aspect of their service.  From the moment I drove up to select my option to when I pulled out of the tunnel and went to use the vacumms.

Needless to say, when passing through the area again, which I often do, I will be back.

< text>
I was so excited to eat here, but unfortunately, it was terrible! I went with my mom and daughter on our little girls trip. We made a reservation for 7:30 on a Sunday evening. The restaurant was beautiful inside and out. Had a table outside with a view of the golf course and misters to keep cool, it was a hot night! We ordered calamari, cold and mushy, crabcakes were extremely fishy tasting with no hard sear on the outside, again cold and mushy, and the wedge salad was probably the best thing we ate all night. For our entr√©es we ordered  2 orders of the "homemade burrata ravioli" and an order of "big zach's bbq ribs". First off we asked the server if she liked the ravioli more or the lobster pizza more. She said the ravioli. I hope she wasn't just trying to upsell. Ravioli were $30 lobster pizza was $20. It was literally frozen ravioli from Costco. No burrata anywhere! It was ricotta. I should have known, ive never heard of burrata ravioli. Usually its eaten as an appetizer with crackers or fruit because its the star of the show. The ravioli was served on top of wilted greens with a tomato coulis sauce on top of the ravioli. The "wilted greens" was a pile of arugula at the bottom of the bowl. It was wilted because they poured hot ravioli on top of it. It was not wilted in a pan with butter or olive oil and garlic or other seasonings. I should have taken a picture of it. It was truly disgusting. Old salad water. Yum. The sauce was hunts tomato sauce from a can. So very disappointing! Also, the server brought two of the meal's out and no joke a full 5 minutes later they finally brought the 3rd. No "I'm sorry". Also, no checking back in a few minutes to see how everything was tasting. The bbq ribs tasted like they had been sitting in a fridge for a week. They had a very strange asian inspired flavor going on, would have been nice if it said that on the menu. It was like plum bbq sauce. Just weird, maybe would have enjoyed it if the ribs weren't a week old. They almost had the texture of tuna fish in a can, the meat flaked off of the bone. I wouldn't have minded paying $160.00 if the food was good. Food was terrible. Service was also terrible. Ambiance was lovely. Also, no joke we were not feeling well that night! Fighting for the bathroom ugh!!<//text>

My husband and I were asked to join our very good friends for dinner at CAMPS on Wednesday night the 16th as part of a birthday celebration.
My husband and I will never go back as our dinner was dreadful.
We had been there about six months ago with family and had a similar experience but decided on Wednesday to give it another chance since so much time had passed. <rate>2< /rate><Pictures>None<//Pictures><GmapID>0x80dbffbc00000001:0x86a3a5d9ac885001</GmapID>< review>
PROS: the guys here are excellent at communication and customer service, very polite and easy to work with. They also take care of your car in a very timely manner, faster than a lot of shops around here do.

CONS: The first time I came here, it was for a rotate and balance. When I drove away, I noticed a loud grating noise, which turned out to be the wheel weights double-stacked and rubbing on the brake calipers. Not a huge issue, I brought it back to them and they fixed it. The next time I came, it was for an oil change. While they were working on it, they called and offered to change the cabin air filter for $50. The filter itself is only about $8, so while I know they have to upcharge to make money, $50 seemed a bit steep. I declined, but when I picked up the car to drive it home, I realized that they never reinstalled the old cabin air filter. It was just sitting on the floorboard, with the cover and glove compartment hanging open and dust everywhere. A few days later, I noticed that there was a consistent oil leak happening (this car has never leaked oil up to this point). I got under the car, check the oil drain plug, and it was completely loose; not even finger-tight. I tightened it up, and the oil leak stopped.

None of these issues are major ones, but it just shows a lack of attention to detail and thoroughness. I like the people who work here, they have great reviews in general, and I want to make this my go-to shop, but will have to find a new place if the work quality stays the same.< /review>
